.oo_tab_ie_right:focus,.oo_tab_ie_right:hover{right:6px;width:40px!important}</style><link type="text/css" rel="stylesheet" href="//williamhill-lang.custhelp.com/euf/assets/css/cp_css.css" /><script type="text/javascript">undefined</script></head><body class="prominent-login-enabled layout-desktop" data-page="matches"><div class="mboxDefault mbox-name-Sportsbook_Trafalgar_Global_Mbox at-element-marker" style="visibility:visible;"></div><script type="text/javascript">var waitFor = function (condition, retryTime, maxRetries, success, failure) {

    failure = failure || function () {};
    var retried = 0;
    var timer = null;

    var waitForImpl = function () {
        if (condition()) {
            window.clearTimeout(timer);
            success();
        } else if (retried &gt; maxRetries) {
            window.clearTimeout(timer);
            failure();
        } else {
            retried++;
            timer = window.setTimeout(waitForImpl, retryTime);
        }
    };

    waitForImpl();
};</script><script type="text/javascript" async="" src="//sports-pp1.staticcache.org/whassets/_cdn/js/sportsbook.js?9ad31748b0c5930ecfa59510fb03ac50"></script><div id="main-off-canvas" if (window.top !== window.self) {
    window.top.location = window.self.location;

var waitFor = function (condition, retryTime, maxRetries, success, failure) {

    failure = failure || function () {};

    var retried = 0;
    var timer = null;

    var waitForImpl = function () {
        if (condition()) {
            window.clearTimeout(timer);
            success();
        } else if (retried &gt; maxRetries) {
            window.clearTimeout(timer);
            failure();
        } else {
            retried++;
            timer = window.setTimeout(waitForImpl, retryTime);
        }
    };

    waitForImpl();
};

var appendScriptTag = function(src, async) {

    var s = document.createElement( 'script' );
    s.setAttribute( 'src', src );
    if (async) {

        s.setAttribute("async", "");
    }
    document.body.appendChild( s );
